core_county_elblag = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation

		available = {
			AND = {
			controls_state = 49
			controls_state = 631
			}
		}

		visible = {
			owns_state = 49
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					49 = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
					631 = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			state = 49
		}

		modifier = {
			stability_weekly = -0.0025
			political_power_gain = -0.15
		}

		cost = 25

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 30
		remove_effect  = {
			add_state_core = 49
			add_state_core = 631
			add_stability = 0.025
		}
	}
